msg:Hyatt is no stranger to the brand, and I am a fan of the brand. My company has also held a dinner party on the 3rd floor of the hotel before, and I think the service and products are quite good.

Lobby: The doorman opens the door to the service unit. During the epidemic period, you need to check the Suikang code before entering.

Front desk: There was only one person on duty at the time, and another person on duty came back to check me in a few minutes later. The staff at the front desk is very fast in handling. For only a few months of business, they are very familiar with the business process and take the initiative to arrange a late check-out for me.

Room: As always, the room type of Regency Club was booked, and it was arranged on the 21st floor of the top floor of the hotel. The room is about 40 square meters, with plenty of space and very good lighting.
Hygiene: Basic hygiene is in place and should be able to satisfy most of the guests.

Regency Club: The executive lounge on the 20th floor is very spacious and has a wide view of the landscape.

Chinese restaurant (3rd floor): I ate lunch at this restaurant for two days. It is conceivable that the products must be excellent, and the service can basically exceed the restaurant standards of many five-star hotels. Especially recommend trying the roast pork and wasabi salad prawn balls, you won't be disappointed.

Surroundings: The neighborhood is under development. There is a Hopson Mall next door, but it is still relatively deserted. It is recommended to travel by car, take a taxi, or walk about 800 meters to the Wanda Plaza. Tired of the hotel's food, of course, take-out is also very convenient, there are take-out tables outside the lobby (self-pickup). Starbucks hasn't opened yet, but there is an IKEA convenience store on the right side of the hotel walking 80 meters.

Suggestions and Reviews (should be carefully considered by hotel management):
1) The room is not equipped with shoe handle, shoe brush and handbag. (basically have more than four stars).
2) In addition to the minibar list, there is no hotel introduction (including restaurant menu/facilities/escape guidelines) in the room. Adding in-room catering will undoubtedly bring additional benefits to the hotel.
3) The toilet lighting is a one-button switch. It is considered that at least two lights are controlled, and it is not necessary to turn off all the lights or brighten them when taking a bath.
4) The bar mirror in the room is oxidized or dirty, see the picture.
5) It is believed that customers can choose whether to pay a deposit or not when checking in, and they can enjoy a 15% discount when registering the house account.
6) The Happy Hour service in Regency Club is obviously lacking, the staffing of waiters is not enough to cope with dining guests, and the service experience has declined. There are few dishes (potatoes are repeated in both dishes), besides soft drinks, coffee, sparkling water and alcohol, it is appropriate to consider adding fruit juice.
7) When the cooling setting is turned on, the wind is set to 3 and 16 degrees, but the temperature in the room cannot be lowered below 25 degrees. Finally, a fan and a window are required to solve the problem.
8) A late check-out has been arranged for me when I checked in, but the front desk still called to the room around 12.45 that day, which was lacking in system remarks and management.
9) The waiter in the Chinese restaurant should wait for the food to be served or after the meal before making a return visit, inquiring about membership and other matters, otherwise the success rate will be almost 0 if the product is unknown.
10) The breakfast is in the form of a buffet with few dishes. In this respect, there is a big gap between the hotels Sofitel and the Grand Hyatt in Huachenghui.

bonus
1) The American organic brand Pharmacopia is a niche brand. The first time I use it, I personally feel that the fragrance and skin feel are good.
2) The service attitude and courtesy of the staff in each post are very good and kind.
3) The Chinese restaurant's products are very good, about 200 per capita, and the price is high. It is worth trying.
4) Double-layer cheesecake YYDS in the lobby bar, 38 yuan a piece, rich in flavor.
5) In the cafeteria on the second floor (breakfast), the waiter has a positive attitude, I asked for an iced latte and it was satisfied because I asked for sugar (give syrup). This is better than many hotels, at least not giving me white sugar.

Summary: The hotel also has an agreement with my company, and I hope that the next visit will be able to improve the stay experience. For Xintang and the surrounding area, Hyatt Regency is definitely a five-star hotel.
